          <h1 class="entry-title">2023-2024 NBA Player Stats</h1>
         </header>
         <div class="entry-content content">
          <hr class="x-hr">
          <nav aria-label="breadcrumbs" class="rank-math-breadcrumb">
           <p><a href="https://www.nbastuffer.com">Home</a><span class="separator"> » </span><a href="https://www.nbastuffer.com/nba-stats/">NBA Stats</a><span class="separator"> » </span><a href="https://www.nbastuffer.com/nba-stats/player/">Player Stats</a><span class="separator"> » </span><span class="last">2023-2024 NBA Player Stats</span></p>
          </nav>
          <div id="" class="x-alert x-alert-info x-alert-block" style="">
           <h6 class="h-alert">Features of Stats Table</h6> 1) Click column headers to sort by <b>NBA stats</b>. Reverse the sort order by clicking on it twice. 
           <br>
            2) Type any name or team in the search box for a quick filter. 
           <br>
            3) To compare, choose more than one player from the player drop-down menu. 
           <br>
            4) Use the “Custom Search Builder” to find players who fit more than one set of criteria at the same time. This tool is useful if you play <b>NBA player prop bets</b>
           <br>
            For example, you can find NBA players who averaged at least 25 points+assists on a 0.500% or higher eFG%, with a usage rate of less than 25% in the 2023-2024 season 
           <br>
            5) There is a glossary at the bottom of the page. 
           <br>
           <hr class="x-gap" style="margin: 10px 0 0 0;"> If you need game-by-game logs, we deliver daily updated <a href="https://www.bigdataball.com/subscribe/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>NBA player datasets</b></a> in Excel throughout the entire season. 
           <br>
          </div>
          <div id="" class="x-alert x-alert-muted x-alert-block" style="">
           <b>Jump to:</b> <a href="#PlayerGlossary">Glossary</a>

          <div id="" class="x-alert x-alert-muted x-alert-block" style="">
           Stats last updated 17 hours ago. Stats include In-Season Tournament games except the Championship game.
          </div>
          <h3><a name="PlayerGlossary">NBA PLAYER STATS GLOSSARY</a></h3>
          <div class="x-columnize">
           <b><u>USG%</u></b>: Usage rate, a.k.a., usage percentage is an estimate of the percentage of team plays used by a player while he was on the floor 
           <br><b><u>TO%</u></b>: A metric that estimates the number of turnovers a player commits per 100 possessions 
           <br><b><u>eFG%</u></b>: With eFG%, three-point shots made are worth 50% more than two-point shots made. eFG% Formula=(FGM+ (0.5 x 3PM))/FGA 
           <br><b><u>TS%</u></b>: True shooting percentage is a measure of shooting efficiency that takes into account field goals, 3-point field goals, and free throws 
           <br><b><u>PPG</u></b>: Points per game 
           <br><b><u>RPG</u></b>: Rebounds per game 
           <br><b><u>APG</u></b>: Assists per game 
           <br><b><u>SPG</u></b>: Steals per game 
           <br><b><u>BPG</u></b>: Blocks per game 
           <br><b><u>TOPG</u></b>: Turnovers per game 
           <br><b><u>P+R</u></b>: Player Props = (Points + Rebounds) total per game 
           <br><b><u>P+A</u></b>: Player Props = (Points + Assists) total per game 
           <br><b><u>P+R+A</u></b>: Player Props = (Points + Rebounds + Assists) total per game 
           <br><b><u>VI</u></b>: The versatility index is a metric that measures a player’s ability to produce in points, assists, and rebounds. The average player will score around a five on the index, while top players score above 10 
           <br><b><u>ORTG</u></b>: Individual offensive rating is the number of points produced by a player per 100 total individual possessions 
           <br><b><u>DRTG</u></b>: Individual defensive rating estimates how many points the player allowed per 100 possessions he individually faced while staying on the court. 
           <br>
          </div>
          <div id="" class="x-alert x-alert-muted x-alert-block" style="">
           <b>Jump to:</b> <a href="#2324PlayerRegSeason">Regular Season Player Stats</a>
          </div>
